)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF 'C' OPTION ON) AS A QUESTION.  THE USER (DA
)@@G@@OR             *******  @H@@@@. ******* OPERATOR) RESPONSE COMPLETES THEDB

)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@@. ******* *END                            DI
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DJ

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* *FILE                       - A MODE 4 TYPE DO
)@@G@@FILE SGS IS    *******  @H@@@@. *******                             -   DP
)@@G@@GENERATED FROM NEXT INPUT  *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DQ

)@@G@@EPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN '*IF LAST ....' STATEMENT,  *******  @H@@@@. ****DS
)@@G@@*** THE STATEMENT BEFORE THE '*IF' STATEMENT IS REPEATED UNTIL *******  DT
)@@G@@@H@@@@. ******* THE CONDITION ON THE '*IF' STATEMENT BECOMES TRUE.      DU
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF A '*REPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN SGS IMAGE, THDV
)@@G@@AT SGS IMAGE   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS REPEATED UNTIL A RESPONSE OF DW
)@@G@@'$END' IS GIVEN.           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DX
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@@. ******* AN ANSWEDY
)@@G@@R OF '$SKIP' TO ANY SGS QUESTION, WILL SKIP        *******  @H@@@@. ****DZ

)@@G@@LLOW THE FIRST (WITH A @EOF*******  @H@@@@. ******* IN BETWEEN), THEY WIEL

)@@G@@TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********                                KS

)@@G@@1       PREASG            . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SET KEY@F@9@8          J RZ
)@@G@@        CONT1             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @F@@@9          J SA
)@@G@@        CONT2             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @E@;@9CONT0     E$SB
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@;@9          E$MSG   SC
)@@G@@  USE @D@;@9          E$DECV    0,,U              . PRESENT CYCLE @#@;@9SD
)@@G@@          E$MSGR  @G@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . '@USE LOSE
)@@G@@G$,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$(0)' @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . '@SF
)@@G@@ASG,AI LOG$'@F@/@;CONT0     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST SG
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @F@@@/CONT1     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST SH
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @ @@@;          L,U       A6,' '    @ @@@;          SLJ     SI
)@@G@@  CYCLE     @D@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT          . GET LEAD ITEM SJ
)@@G@@@H@@@9                                      . CHANGE MSCON PKT TO READ MSK
)@@G@@AIN ITEM    @E@@@9          SP1,S3    MSCONPKT+3        .   FOR LATER CASL
)@@G@@LLS   @G@@@9          L,S4      A0,BUFFER+9       . CALCULATE OLDEST RELSM
)@@G@@ CYCLE-1    @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@C@@@9          SN        A0,LSN
)@@G@@OGCYCLE       . STORE   @E@9@8CONT0     LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GESO
)@@G@@T NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@/@9CONT1     LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXTSP
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@/          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CSQ
)@@G@@YCLE  @C@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR   @F@9@8CONT1 SR
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,READ          . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@9CONT2 SS
)@@G@@    LMJ       X9,READ           . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@8      ST
)@@G@@    L         A0,0,X5           . CHECK FOR END OF CYCLE    @ @@@8      SU
)@@G@@    TNE       A0,(-0)   @C@9@8          J         CONT7             . YESV
)@@G@@S     @C@@@9          J         CONT11            . YES     @H@@@8      SW
)@@G@@    TE        A0,SENTINEL       . CHECK FOR LAST TAPE BLOCK SENTINEL    SX
)@@G@@@^@@@8          J         $+3 @G@9@8          SZ        FIRST           SY
)@@G@@  . INITIALIZE FIRST TIME THRU FLAG @F@@@9          SZ        FIRST     SZ
)@@G@@        . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8          J         EXIT      TA
)@@G@@        . END OF TAPE   @G@@@8          L         A0,STIME          . CHTB
)@@G@@ECK STARTING TIME IF SPECIFIED@ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT2  @ @@@9TC
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,CONT3  @D@@@8          L         A1,LLOGT        TD
)@@G@@  . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDATE            . COMPARE TE
)@@G@@WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60          . IF STIME MORE TF
)@@G@@THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,60*60          . IF STIMETG
)@@G@@ MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@8          TP        A3                .   TH
)@@G@@FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZ        NBUF            TI
)@@G@@  . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  TJ
)@@G@@        . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8          JN        A2,CTK
)@@G@@ONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9          JN        A2,CTL
)@@G@@ONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9CONT3     TZ        PRIVTM
)@@G@@              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9          J         CONT4     TN
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,('EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIPTO
)@@G@@ EXEC 8 ENTRIES   @ @@@9          TNE       A0,LRUNID @ @@@9          J TP
)@@G@@        CONT2     @F@9@8CONT2     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUTQ
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @F@@@9CONT4     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUTR
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @G@9@8          JZ        A0,CONT4          .    IGNORTS
)@@G@@ING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @G@@@9          JZ        A0,CONT7          .   TT
)@@G@@ IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @^@@@8          L,U       X4,5@ @9@8CONT2ATU
)@@G@@    EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@9CONT5     EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@8      TV
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A0,'-'    @ @9@8          J         CONT3     @ @@@9      TW
)@@G@@    J         CONT6     @ @@@8          EX        TEST,X4   @ @9@8      TX
)@@G@@    J         CONT3     @ @@@9          J         CONT6     @^@9@8      TY
)@@G@@    SZ        NBUF@ @@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  @ @9@8          J TZ
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @ @9@8CONT3     JGUA
)@@G@@D       X4,CONT2A @ @@@9CONT6     JGD       X4,CONT5  @F@9@8CONT4     L UB
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @F@@@9CONT7     L UC
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          L,UD
)@@G@@H2      A0,0,A1   @F@@@8          TNZ,H1    0,X10             . CHECK IFUE
)@@G@@ TYPE TABLE INPUT @E@9@8          J         CONT4A            . NO, JUSTUF
)@@G@@ ONE TYPE   @E@@@9          J         CONT8             . NO, JUST ONE TUG
)@@G@@YPE   @F@@@8          L,H1      R1,0,X10          . SCAN TYPE TABLE FOR UH
)@@G@@MATCH @ @@@8          L         X1,0,X10  @^@@@8          LXI,U     X1,1UI
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,LTYPE  @ @@@8          SE,H2     A0,0,*X1  UJ
)@@G@@@E@9@8          J         CONT1             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @E@@@9UK
)@@G@@          J         CONT2             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@9@8      UL
)@@G@@    J         CONT5             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @F@@@9      UM
)@@G@@    J         CONT9             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @E@9@8CONT4AUN
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT5          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @E@@@9CONT8     JZUO
)@@G@@        A0,CONT9          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          TE      UP
)@@G@@  A0,LTYPE  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J       UQ
)@@G@@  CONT2     @G@9@8CONT5     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEARCH KUR
)@@G@@EY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEUS
)@@G@@ARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT6  @ @@@9      UT
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ        WDNO              . ISUU
)@@G@@ WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A            . NO, PLAIN SEARUV
)@@G@@CH KEY SPECIFIED  @G@@@9          L         X1,X5             . YES, STRUW
)@@G@@ING SEARCH SPECIFIED    @ @@@9          L,H2      X2,3,X10  @ @@@9      UX
)@@G@@    L,U       A1,24*6   @^@@@9          L,U       A2,6@A@@@9          LMUY
)@@G@@J       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@9          J         CONT2             . NOUZ
)@@G@@ FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@@@9          J         CONT10            . STRING FVA
)@@G@@OUND, CONTINUE    @ @9@8          L         X4,WDNO   @ @@@9CONT9A    L VB
)@@G@@        X4,WDNO   @ @@@8          A         X4,X5     @ @@@8          L VC
)@@G@@        A1,0,X4   @ @@@8          TE        A1,A0     @ @9@8          J VD
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @F@9@8CONT6     L,VE
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@F@@@9CONT10    L,VF
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@ @@@8          L,VG
)@@G@@U       X4,BUFF   @^@@@8          LXI,U     X4,1@ @@@8          L       VH
)@@G@@  X6,X5     @^@@@8          LXI,U     X6,1@ @@@8          BT        X4,0VI
)@@G@@,*X6  @E@@@8          S         X5,POINTER        . SAME BLOCK POINTER  VJ
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RETURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNVK
)@@G@@Z       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     VL
)@@G@@@I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FVM
)@@G@@ILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GET NEXTVN
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@9          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CVO
)@@G@@YCLE  @H@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR - FINISHED SEAVP
)@@G@@RCH (NO FIND)     @C@9@8          J         CONT1             . CONTINUEVQ
)@@G@@@C@@@9          J         CONT2             . CONTINUE@F@@@8EXIT      TZVR
)@@G@@,S1     0,X10             . CHECK FOR FOR V OR FTN    @C@@@8          J VS
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FTN     @C@@@8          J         6,X10     VT
)@@G@@        . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********************************VU
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@8. *******              RVV
)@@G@@EAD LOG ENTRY SUBROUTINE                     *******  @H@@@8. **********VW
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@8VX
)@@G@@.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ        NBUF              . ISVY
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ        ENTRYNUM          . ISVZ
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J         READ3             . NOWA
)@@G@@@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YES, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESWB
)@@G@@S BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8@ @@@8READ1     S       WC
)@@G@@  A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP             . READ NEXT 224 WD
)@@G@@WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   @C@@@8          J       WE
)@@G@@  READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INC       NBLOCKS         WF
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOP     @E@@@8          L WG
)@@G@@        A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   @ @@@8          TE      WH
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2             . NO@G@@@8      WI
)@@G@@    L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOR ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9WJ
)@@G@@          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PRESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   WK
)@@G@@@G@@@8          J         READ1             . GO BACK AND READ THAT SECTWL
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER         . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFEWM
)@@G@@RS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ           . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO WN
)@@G@@ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  @F@9@8          L,U     WO
)@@G@@  A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@F@@@9          SP1     WP
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@A@9@8          S       WQ
)@@G@@  A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 @G@@@8READ3     SZ      WR
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    @F@9@8          L WS
)@@G@@        A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @F@@@9          L WT
)@@G@@        A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @^@@@8          AUWU
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     @ @@@8          A,U     WV
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     @F@@@8          TG      WW
)@@G@@  A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    @^@@@8          SZ      WX
)@@G@@  A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9          S         A1,EWY
)@@G@@NTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @F@@@9WZ
)@@G@@          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENT NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9XA
)@@G@@          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9              . RETURN  XB
)@@G@@@F@@@8READE     .                           . CLEAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   XC
)@@G@@@E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8XD
)@@G@@          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J         EXIT              . NOXE
)@@G@@T EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$      READP             . REXF
)@@G@@AD NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3           . I/O ERROXG
)@@G@@R?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT              . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLEXH
)@@G@@ EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3        . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFEXI
)@@G@@R READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8          J         EXITXJ
)@@G@@              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          L         A0,(054160XK
)@@G@@0000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8          TE        A0,BXL
)@@G@@UFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    XM
)@@G@@@G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLEAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TAXN
)@@G@@PES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************XO
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@8. ****XP
)@@G@@******           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                 *******  XQ
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************XR
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8          CSF$      FREEXS
)@@G@@,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSF$      FREE,NFREE      XT
)@@G@@  . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CYCLE          . IS CYCLEXU
)@@G@@ = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE          . INCREMENT LOGCXV
)@@G@@YCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'            . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9XW
)@@G@@          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYCLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8XX
)@@G@@          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          AN,U      A1,1            XY
)@@G@@  . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CYCLE  @E@'@9          E$XZ
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@'@9          E$MSG   YA
)@@G@@  USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     @A@@@'          L       YB
)@@G@@  A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1@^@@@'          A,U     YC
)@@G@@  A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'          SLJ       CYCLYD
)@@G@@E             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9          E$DECV  @#@;@9      YE
)@@G@@    E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE          . @USE MASTER,SYYF
)@@G@@S$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . @USE LOGYG
)@@G@@$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A MYH
)@@G@@ASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8YI
)@@G@@          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9      YJ
)@@G@@    TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANT MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    YK
)@@G@@@B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NO@G@@@9          MSCON$  YL
)@@G@@  MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOG FILE @E@@@9          E$YM
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     @D@@@9          E$FD2   YN
)@@G@@  BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9YO
)@@G@@          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAME     @^@@@9          E$YP
)@@G@@CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,,T3     . ABS CYCLE     YQ
)@@G@@@^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     YR
)@@G@@@^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$DECV                    YS
)@@G@@  . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9          E$DAY3    BUFFYT
)@@G@@ER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9YU
)@@G@@          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1           YV
)@@G@@  . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT                     . PRINT SUYW
)@@G@@MMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   YX
)@@G@@@G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAS A START TIME SPECIFIEDYY
)@@G@@?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX             . NO@B@@@;          J YZ
)@@G@@        NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,U       A5,1            ZA
)@@G@@  . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,U       A6,'1'          ZB
)@@G@@  .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ       CYCLE     @H@@@'      ZC
)@@G@@    JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH THAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    ZD
)@@G@@@F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GET MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    ZE
)@@G@@@G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COMPARE START TIME WITH CYZF
)@@G@@CLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19      .    CATALOGUE TIME   ZG
)@@G@@@H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IF START TIME > CATALOGUE ZH
)@@G@@TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA          .    PRESENT CYCZI
)@@G@@LE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT           .    PRESENT CYCLE    ZJ
)@@G@@@F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZK
)@@G@@@F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZL
)@@G@@@F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZM
)@@G@@@ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8          SZ        NBUF      ZN
)@@G@@        . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRZO
)@@G@@YNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @C@9@8          J       ZP
)@@G@@  1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J         1,X9            ZQ
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************************************ZR
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@'. ******* ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBZS
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@'. *******         ZT
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@'. ****ZU
)@@G@@*** INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                                     *******  ZV
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX                                ZW
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. *******                                             ZX
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. ****************************************ZY
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@'CYCLE     +         0   @E@@@'ZZ
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USE' IMAGE    @D@@@'      AA
)@@G@@    E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  @D@@@'          E$FD1   AB
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'          E$MSGR              AC
)@@G@@        . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5                . REL CYCLAD
)@@G@@E     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFAE
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT      AF
)@@G@@        . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$MSG     ASG             AG
)@@G@@  . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOAH
)@@G@@G$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT ASG IMAAI
)@@G@@GE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE            . RETURN  @[@@@'.     AJ
)@@G@@@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************************************AK
)@@G@@*********************** @H@@@8. *******                                 AL
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* TDATE TIME DIFFERENCAM
)@@G@@E SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@8. *******         AN
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****AO
)@@G@@*** WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77                            *******  AP
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         AQ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILL CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFAR
)@@G@@ERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONDS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPAS
)@@G@@RESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. *******                     AT
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* INPUTS AAU
)@@G@@RE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.      *******  @H@@@8. ****AV
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  AW
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************AX
)@@G@@************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATE*   +         0         AY
)@@G@@        . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DS        A0,DTDIN        AZ
)@@G@@  . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DTDIN          . CHECK IFBA
)@@G@@ MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TE,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8BB
)@@G@@          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO BAD   @F@@@8          L BC
)@@G@@        A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATION     @ @@@8          ANBD
)@@G@@        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . ALL DONEBE
)@@G@@@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964BF
)@@G@@, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP        . SAVE CONVERTED TIME BG
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8          SLJ       DTDSUB    BH
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          AN        A0,DBI
)@@G@@TDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8          L         A2,A0     BJ
)@@G@@        . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DL        A0,DTDIN        BK
)@@G@@  . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . DONE    BL
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************BM
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO SECONDS SINCE 1964      BN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************BO
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@8DTDSUB    +         0   @D@@@8BP
)@@G@@          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPUT    @^@@@8          SZBQ
)@@G@@        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8BR
)@@G@@          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          AN,U      A3,1@ @@@8      BS

)@@G@@        X=0 , END @H@@@@MY        EQU       +(W (DIU(0,1)--DIU(0,1)*/-72PH
)@@G@@)+0377777777777*(DIU(0,1)=0)) @ @@@@MBETA     EQU       MY-MY/X*X @A@@@@PI
)@@G@@Y1        EQU       MY/(X-MBETA)    @ @@@@Y2        EQU       MY-MBETA-1PJ
)@@G@@@E@@@@ . DECIDE WHICH VALUE OF (ALPHA*Y)/(X-BETA) WILL BE LARGER. @C@@@@PK
)@@G@@ . THE LARGER VALUE WILL BE: (ALPHA*NUM) / DNM. @C@@@@NUM       EQU     PL
)@@G@@  (Y1<Y2)*Y2+MY*(Y1>Y2-1)     @C@@@@DNM       EQU       (X-MBETA-1)*(Y1>PM

)@@G@@@^@@@@ALPHA(0)  EQU       X-1 @#@@@@TOP       NAME    @D@@@@N(0)      EQPO
)@@G@@U       N(0)+1.             TRY THE NEXT N@C@@@@F(0)      EQU       F(0)PP

)@@G@@LPHA(0)-X*(ALPHA(0)*2>X-1)+ALPHA(0) @D@@@@          DO        1+ALPHA(0)PR
)@@G@@*NUM>DNM*/N(0) , GO TOP @ @@@@N(1)      EQU       N(0)+1    @#@@@@DECN  PS
)@@G@@    NAME    @ @@@@N(1)      EQU       N(1)-1    @C@@@@          DO      PT
)@@G@@  N(1)<N(0) ,F(0) EQU F(0)*/-1@B@@@@          DO        F(0)**1=0 , GO DPU
)@@G@@ECN   @A@@@@OPT       EQU       F(0)>1D*/35-1   @B@@@@          DO      PV
)@@G@@  OPT , DSA DIU(1,1),36 @E@@@@          DO        OPT , DI DIU(1,1),+(OPPW
)@@G@@T$$ DIU(1,2))     @ @@@@OPT0      EQU       F(0)=1    @E@@@@          DOPX

)@@G@@EM MASTER LOG  *******  @H@@@9. ******* FILE ON MASS STORAGE.           TG

)@@G@@AD             *******  @H@@@8. *******      - DON'T LEAVE ANY MASS STORUI

)@@G@@NG BLOCK       *******  @H@@@9. *******      - EXTERNALIZE TAG 'PRINTCYCUW

)@@G@@          E$MSGR  @G@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . '@USE LOWD
)@@G@@G$,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$(0)' @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . '@WE
)@@G@@ASG,AI LOG$'@F@/@;CONT0     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST WF
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @F@@@/CONT1     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST WG
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @ @@@;          L,U       A6,' '    @ @@@;          SLJ     WH
)@@G@@  CYCLE     @D@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT          . GET LEAD ITEM WI
)@@G@@@H@@@9                                      . CHANGE MSCON PKT TO READ MWJ
)@@G@@AIN ITEM    @E@@@9          SP1,S3    MSCONPKT+3        .   FOR LATER CAWK
)@@G@@LLS   @G@@@9          L,S4      A0,BUFFER+9       . CALCULATE OLDEST RELWL
)@@G@@ CYCLE-1    @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@C@@@9          SN        A0,LWM
)@@G@@OGCYCLE       . STORE   @E@9@8CONT0     LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GEWN
)@@G@@T NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@/@9CONT1     LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXTWO
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@/          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CWP
)@@G@@YCLE  @C@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR   @F@9@8CONT1 WQ
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,READ          . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@9CONT2 WR
)@@G@@    LMJ       X9,READ           . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@8      WS
)@@G@@    L         A0,0,X5           . CHECK FOR END OF CYCLE    @ @@@8      WT
)@@G@@    TNE       A0,(-0)   @C@9@8          J         CONT7             . YEWU
)@@G@@S     @C@@@9          J         CONT11            . YES     @H@@@8      WV
)@@G@@    TE        A0,SENTINEL       . CHECK FOR LAST TAPE BLOCK SENTINEL    WW
)@@G@@@^@@@8          J         $+3 @G@9@8          SZ        FIRST           WX
)@@G@@  . INITIALIZE FIRST TIME THRU FLAG @F@@@9          SZ        FIRST     WY
)@@G@@        . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8          J         EXIT      WZ
)@@G@@        . END OF TAPE   @G@@@8          L         A0,STIME          . CHXA
)@@G@@ECK STARTING TIME IF SPECIFIED@ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT2  @ @@@9XB
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,CONT3  @D@@@8          L         A1,LLOGT        XC
)@@G@@  . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDATE            . COMPARE XD
)@@G@@WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60          . IF STIME MORE XE
)@@G@@THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,60*60          . IF STIMEXF
)@@G@@ MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@8          TP        A3                .   XG
)@@G@@FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZ        NBUF            XH
)@@G@@  . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  XI
)@@G@@        . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8          JN        A2,CXJ
)@@G@@ONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9          JN        A2,CXK
)@@G@@ONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9CONT3     TZ        PRIVXL
)@@G@@              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9          J         CONT4     XM
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,('EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIPXN
)@@G@@ EXEC 8 ENTRIES   @ @@@9          TNE       A0,LRUNID @ @@@9          J XO
)@@G@@        CONT2     @F@9@8CONT2     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUXP
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @F@@@9CONT4     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUXQ
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @G@9@8          JZ        A0,CONT4          .    IGNORXR
)@@G@@ING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @G@@@9          JZ        A0,CONT7          .   XS
)@@G@@ IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @^@@@8          L,U       X4,5@ @9@8CONT2AXT
)@@G@@    EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@9CONT5     EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@8      XU
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A0,'-'    @ @9@8          J         CONT3     @ @@@9      XV
)@@G@@    J         CONT6     @ @@@8          EX        TEST,X4   @ @9@8      XW
)@@G@@    J         CONT3     @ @@@9          J         CONT6     @^@9@8      XX
)@@G@@    SZ        NBUF@ @@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  @ @9@8          J XY
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @ @9@8CONT3     JGXZ
)@@G@@D       X4,CONT2A @ @@@9CONT6     JGD       X4,CONT5  @F@9@8CONT4     L YA
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @F@@@9CONT7     L YB
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          L,YC
)@@G@@H2      A0,0,A1   @F@@@8          TNZ,H1    0,X10             . CHECK IFYD
)@@G@@ TYPE TABLE INPUT @E@9@8          J         CONT4A            . NO, JUSTYE
)@@G@@ ONE TYPE   @E@@@9          J         CONT8             . NO, JUST ONE TYF
)@@G@@YPE   @F@@@8          L,H1      R1,0,X10          . SCAN TYPE TABLE FOR YG
)@@G@@MATCH @ @@@8          L         X1,0,X10  @^@@@8          LXI,U     X1,1YH
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,LTYPE  @ @@@8          SE,H2     A0,0,*X1  YI
)@@G@@@E@9@8          J         CONT1             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @E@@@9YJ
)@@G@@          J         CONT2             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@9@8      YK
)@@G@@    J         CONT5             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @F@@@9      YL
)@@G@@    J         CONT9             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @E@9@8CONT4AYM
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT5          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @E@@@9CONT8     JZYN
)@@G@@        A0,CONT9          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          TE      YO
)@@G@@  A0,LTYPE  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J       YP
)@@G@@  CONT2     @G@9@8CONT5     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEARCH KYQ
)@@G@@EY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEYR
)@@G@@ARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT6  @ @@@9      YS
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ        WDNO              . ISYT
)@@G@@ WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A            . NO, PLAIN SEARYU
)@@G@@CH KEY SPECIFIED  @G@@@9          L         X1,X5             . YES, STRYV
)@@G@@ING SEARCH SPECIFIED    @ @@@9          L,H2      X2,3,X10  @ @@@9      YW
)@@G@@    L,U       A1,24*6   @^@@@9          L,U       A2,6@A@@@9          LMYX
)@@G@@J       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@9          J         CONT2             . NOYY
)@@G@@ FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@@@9          J         CONT10            . STRING FYZ
)@@G@@OUND, CONTINUE    @ @9@8          L         X4,WDNO   @ @@@9CONT9A    L ZA
)@@G@@        X4,WDNO   @ @@@8          A         X4,X5     @ @@@8          L ZB
)@@G@@        A1,0,X4   @ @@@8          TE        A1,A0     @ @9@8          J ZC
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @F@9@8CONT6     L,ZD
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@F@@@9CONT10    L,ZE
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@ @@@8          L,ZF
)@@G@@U       X4,BUFF   @^@@@8          LXI,U     X4,1@ @@@8          L       ZG
)@@G@@  X6,X5     @^@@@8          LXI,U     X6,1@ @@@8          BT        X4,0ZH
)@@G@@,*X6  @E@@@8          S         X5,POINTER        . SAME BLOCK POINTER  ZI
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RETURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNZJ
)@@G@@Z       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     ZK
)@@G@@@I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FZL
)@@G@@ILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GET NEXTZM
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@9          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CZN
)@@G@@YCLE  @H@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR - FINISHED SEAZO
)@@G@@RCH (NO FIND)     @C@9@8          J         CONT1             . CONTINUEZP
)@@G@@@C@@@9          J         CONT2             . CONTINUE@F@@@8EXIT      TZZQ
)@@G@@,S1     0,X10             . CHECK FOR FOR V OR FTN    @C@@@8          J ZR
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FTN     @C@@@8          J         6,X10     ZS
)@@G@@        . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********************************ZT
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@8. *******              RZU
)@@G@@EAD LOG ENTRY SUBROUTINE                     *******  @H@@@8. **********ZV
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@8ZW
)@@G@@.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ        NBUF              . ISZX
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ        ENTRYNUM          . ISZY
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J         READ3             . NOZZ
)@@G@@@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YES, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESAA
)@@G@@S BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8@ @@@8READ1     S       AB
)@@G@@  A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP             . READ NEXT 224 AC
)@@G@@WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   @C@@@8          J       AD
)@@G@@  READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INC       NBLOCKS         AE
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOP     @E@@@8          L AF
)@@G@@        A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   @ @@@8          TE      AG
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2             . NO@G@@@8      AH
)@@G@@    L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOR ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9AI
)@@G@@          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PRESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   AJ
)@@G@@@G@@@8          J         READ1             . GO BACK AND READ THAT SECTAK
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER         . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFEAL
)@@G@@RS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ           . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO AM
)@@G@@ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  @F@9@8          L,U     AN
)@@G@@  A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@F@@@9          SP1     AO
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@A@9@8          S       AP
)@@G@@  A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 @G@@@8READ3     SZ      AQ
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    @F@9@8          L AR
)@@G@@        A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @F@@@9          L AS
)@@G@@        A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @^@@@8          AUAT
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     @ @@@8          A,U     AU
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     @F@@@8          TG      AV
)@@G@@  A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    @^@@@8          SZ      AW
)@@G@@  A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9          S         A1,EAX
)@@G@@NTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @F@@@9AY
)@@G@@          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENT NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9AZ
)@@G@@          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9              . RETURN  BA
)@@G@@@F@@@8READE     .                           . CLEAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   BB
)@@G@@@E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8BC
)@@G@@          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J         EXIT              . NOBD
)@@G@@T EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$      READP             . REBE
)@@G@@AD NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3           . I/O ERROBF
)@@G@@R?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT              . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLEBG
)@@G@@ EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3        . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFEBH
)@@G@@R READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8          J         EXITBI
)@@G@@              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          L         A0,(054160BJ
)@@G@@0000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8          TE        A0,BBK
)@@G@@UFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    BL
)@@G@@@G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLEAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TABM
)@@G@@PES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************BN
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@8. ****BO
)@@G@@******           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                 *******  BP
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************BQ
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8          CSF$      FREEBR
)@@G@@,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSF$      FREE,NFREE      BS
)@@G@@  . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CYCLE          . IS CYCLEBT
)@@G@@ = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE          . INCREMENT LOGCBU
)@@G@@YCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'            . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9BV
)@@G@@          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYCLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8BW
)@@G@@          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          AN,U      A1,1            BX
)@@G@@  . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CYCLE  @E@'@9          E$BY
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@'@9          E$MSG   BZ
)@@G@@  USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     @A@@@'          L       CA
)@@G@@  A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1@^@@@'          A,U     CB
)@@G@@  A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'          SLJ       CYCLCC
)@@G@@E             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9          E$DECV  @#@;@9      CD
)@@G@@    E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE          . @USE MASTER,SYCE
)@@G@@S$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . @USE LOGCF
)@@G@@$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A MCG
)@@G@@ASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8CH
)@@G@@          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9      CI
)@@G@@    TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANT MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    CJ
)@@G@@@B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NO@G@@@9          MSCON$  CK
)@@G@@  MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOG FILE @E@@@9          E$CL
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     @D@@@9          E$FD2   CM
)@@G@@  BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9CN
)@@G@@          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAME     @^@@@9          E$CO
)@@G@@CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,,T3     . ABS CYCLE     CP
)@@G@@@^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     CQ
)@@G@@@^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$DECV                    CR
)@@G@@  . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9          E$DAY3    BUFFCS
)@@G@@ER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9CT
)@@G@@          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1           CU
)@@G@@  . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT                     . PRINT SUCV
)@@G@@MMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   CW
)@@G@@@G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAS A START TIME SPECIFIEDCX
)@@G@@?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX             . NO@B@@@;          J CY
)@@G@@        NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,U       A5,1            CZ
)@@G@@  . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,U       A6,'1'          DA
)@@G@@  .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ       CYCLE     @H@@@'      DB
)@@G@@    JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH THAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    DC
)@@G@@@F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GET MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    DD
)@@G@@@G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COMPARE START TIME WITH CYDE
)@@G@@CLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19      .    CATALOGUE TIME   DF
)@@G@@@H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IF START TIME > CATALOGUE DG
)@@G@@TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA          .    PRESENT CYCDH
)@@G@@LE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT           .    PRESENT CYCLE    DI
)@@G@@@F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   DJ
)@@G@@@F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   DK
)@@G@@@F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   DL
)@@G@@@ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8          SZ        NBUF      DM
)@@G@@        . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRDN
)@@G@@YNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @C@9@8          J       DO
)@@G@@  1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J         1,X9            DP
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************************************DQ
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@'. ******* ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBDR
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@'. *******         DS
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@'. ****DT
)@@G@@*** INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                                     *******  DU
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX                                DV
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. *******                                             DW
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. ****************************************DX
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@'CYCLE     +         0   @E@@@'DY
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USE' IMAGE    @D@@@'      DZ
)@@G@@    E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  @D@@@'          E$FD1   EA
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'          E$MSGR              EB
)@@G@@        . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5                . REL CYCLEC
)@@G@@E     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFED
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT      EE
)@@G@@        . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$MSG     ASG             EF
)@@G@@  . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOEG
)@@G@@G$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT ASG IMAEH
)@@G@@GE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE            . RETURN  @[@@@'.     EI
)@@G@@@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************************************EJ
)@@G@@*********************** @H@@@8. *******                                 EK
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* TDATE TIME DIFFERENCEL
)@@G@@E SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@8. *******         EM
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****EN
)@@G@@*** WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77                            *******  EO
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         EP
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILL CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFEQ
)@@G@@ERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONDS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPER
)@@G@@RESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. *******                     ES
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* INPUTS AET
)@@G@@RE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.      *******  @H@@@8. ****EU
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  EV
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************EW
)@@G@@************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATE*   +         0         EX
)@@G@@        . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DS        A0,DTDIN        EY
)@@G@@  . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DTDIN          . CHECK IFEZ
)@@G@@ MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TE,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8FA
)@@G@@          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO BAD   @F@@@8          L FB
)@@G@@        A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATION     @ @@@8          ANFC
)@@G@@        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . ALL DONEFD
)@@G@@@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964FE
)@@G@@, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP        . SAVE CONVERTED TIME FF
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8          SLJ       DTDSUB    FG
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          AN        A0,DFH
)@@G@@TDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8          L         A2,A0     FI
)@@G@@        . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DL        A0,DTDIN        FJ
)@@G@@  . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . DONE    FK
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************FL
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO SECONDS SINCE 1964      FM
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************FN
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@8DTDSUB    +         0   @D@@@8FO
)@@G@@          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPUT    @^@@@8          SZFP
)@@G@@        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8FQ
)@@G@@          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          AN,U      A3,1@ @@@8      FR
)@@G@@    L         A0,A3     @E@@@8          DI,U      A2,4              . CHFS
)@@G@@ECK FOR LEAP YEARS@^@@@8          A,U       A2,1@A@@@8          MSI,U   FT
)@@G@@  A2,60*60*24     @B@@@8          MSI       A0,(60*60*24*365)     @ @@@8FU
)@@G@@          A         A0,A2     @C@@@8DTDSC1    L,S1      A2,DTDTEMP+1    FV
)@@G@@  . MONTH   @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@A@@@8DTDSC2    A         A0,DFW
)@@G@@TDTAB,A2    @ @@@8          JGD       A2,DTDSC2 @C@@@8          L,S2    FX
)@@G@@  A2,DTDTEMP+1      . DAY     @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@E@@@8      FY
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A2,60*60*24       . CONVERT TO SECS     @D@@@8          A FZ
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  @G@@@8          L,S3      A3,DGA
)@@G@@TDTEMP+1       . IF LEAP YEAR AND MONTH>FEB,    @H@@@8          AND,U   GB
)@@G@@  A3,3              .    ADD AN EXTRA DAY TO CALCULATION    @ @@@8      GC
)@@G@@    JNZ       A4,DTDSC3 @A@@@8          L,S1      A3,DTDTEMP+1    @^@@@8GD
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A3,3@ @@@8          J         DTDSC3    @A@@@8      GE
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,60*60*24     @C@@@8DTDSC3    L,H2      A2,DTDTEMP+1    GF
)@@G@@  . SECS    @D@@@8          A         A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  GG
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         *DTDSUB           . RETURN  @C@9@8DTDIN     REGH
)@@G@@S       2                 . INPUT   @C@@@9DTDIN     $RES      2         GI
)@@G@@        . INPUT   @^@9@8DTDTEMP   RES       2   @^@@@9DTDTEMP   $RES    GJ
)@@G@@  2   @^@@@8DTDTAB    +         0   @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*3GK
)@@G@@1     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*28     @A@@@8          +       GL
)@@G@@  60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8      GM
)@@G@@    +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     GN
)@@G@@@A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*6GO
)@@G@@0*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8          + GP
)@@G@@        60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @[@@@8GQ
)@@G@@/.    @H@@@8. **********************************************************GR
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@8. **********           D A T A                  GS
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@8. **********************************GT
)@@G@@****************************************  @[@@@8.     @]@9@8$(0)      . GU
)@@G@@@F@9@8NEWBLOCK* RES       1                 . NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    GV
)@@G@@@G@9@8NBUF      RES       1                 . NO. OF ENTRIES IN LOG BLOCGW
)@@G@@K     @[@@@9$(0)  @ @/@8PF        FORM      12,6,18   @^@9@8POINTER   REGX
)@@G@@S       1   @^@@@9POINTER   $RES      1   @^@9@8FIRST     RES       1   GY
)@@G@@@^@@@9FIRST     $RES      1   @ @9@8BUFF      EQUF      *4,X10    @ @@@9GZ
)@@G@@BUFF      $EQUF     *4,X10    @ @9@8STIME     EQUF      *2,X10    @ @@@9HA
)@@G@@STIME     $EQUF     *2,X10    @ @9@8RUNID     EQUF      *1,X10    @ @@@9HB
)@@G@@RUNID     $EQUF     *1,X10    @ @9@8TYPE      EQUF      0,X10,H2  @ @@@9HC
)@@G@@TYPE      $EQUF     0,X10,H2  @ @9@8KEY       EQUF      *3,X10,H2 @ @@@9HD
)@@G@@KEY       $EQUF     *3,X10    @ @9@8WDNO      EQUF      *3,X10,H1 @ @@@9HE
)@@G@@WDNO      $EQUF     3,X10,H1  @F@9@8MNBUF     RES       1               HF
)@@G@@  . MAX NO. OF LOG ENTRIES    @F@@@9MNBUF     $RES      1               HG

)@@G@@        A1,X2     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATEPR
)@@G@@ J1   @ @@@C          L         J1,A1     @ @@@C          L         J2,(PS
)@@G@@1*/35)@ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@C          L,U       SR2,PT
)@@G@@0     @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     @^@@@C          LSSL      A1,9PU
)@@G@@@ @@@C          A         A1,A0     @ @@@C          LSSL      A1,18     PV
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L         SR3,A1    @E@@@C          L,H1      A1,BASCII PW
)@@G@@        . GET INPUT ASCII KEY @H@@@C          L,U       X3,*CONVT,A1    PX
)@@G@@  . GET CORRESPONDING TRANSLATE TABLE     @G@@@C          XOR,H2    A1,BPY
)@@G@@ASCII         . COMPARE TO OUTPUT ASCII KEY     @H@@@C          EX      PZ
)@@G@@  BMOVET,A2         . DO 'BM' IF KEYS =, OTHERWISE DO 'BMT' @F@@@C      QA
)@@G@@    DL        A1,SBMOVE         . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @A@@@C      QB
)@@G@@    L         X3,SBMOVE+2     @C@@@C          J         0,X11           QC
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@B. ****************************************QD
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE GET SUBROUTINE QE
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. *******         QF
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****QG
)@@G@@*** INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  QH
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE                                       QI
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                                             QJ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BGET  QK
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******                     QL
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. ****************QM
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @[@@@CBGET* QN
)@@G@@@E@@@C          DS        A1,SBGET          . SAVE REGISTER USED  @F@@@CQO
)@@G@@          SPD       A0                . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@CQP
)@@G@@          OR,U      A0,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@ @@@C          L QQ
)@@G@@        A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLQR
)@@G@@J       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          S         A1,JQS
)@@G@@0     @C@@@C          L,4       A0,0,*X1          . GET BYTE@F@@@C      QT
)@@G@@    SPD       A1                . TURN OFF CHARACTER MODE   @^@@@C      QU
)@@G@@    AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@F@@@C          DL      QV
)@@G@@  A1,SBGET          . RESTORE REGISTER USED     @ @@@C          J       QW
)@@G@@  0,X11     @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************************QX
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@C@B. *******                     QY
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@C@B. *******     BYTEQZ
)@@G@@ TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE (FIELDATA)                  *******  @H@@@C. ****RA
)@@G@@*** BYTE TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE                                 *******  RB
)@@G@@@H@@@B. *******                                                         RC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)    RD
)@@G@@               *******  @H@C@B. *******     INPUT:  X1 - INPUT BASE ADDRRE
)@@G@@ESS                        *******  @H@C@B. *******             A1 - BYTRF
)@@G@@E # OF INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@C@B. *******         RG
)@@G@@    A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES                          *******  @H@@@C. ****RH
)@@G@@***         A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES                              *******  RI
)@@G@@@^@C@B. *******     OUTPUT: A2@H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A2                RJ
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. *******               RK
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* CARL
)@@G@@LLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BINT                             *******  @H@@@CRM
)@@G@@. *******                   J ILLEGAL-INTEGER                        ***RN
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                   J NORMAL                        RO
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@B. *******                                       RP
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@B. **********************************RQ
)@@G@@****************************************  @^@C@BBINT*     +         0   RR
)@@G@@@[@@@CBINT* @E@C@B          S         A3,SAVE           . SAVE REGISTERSRS
)@@G@@ USED @E@@@C          DS        A0,SBINT           . SAVE REGISTERS USEDRT
)@@G@@@ @@@C          S         X1,SBINT+2@A@@@C          S         X10,SBINT+RU
)@@G@@3     @G@@@C          L,U       X10,1,X11         . SETUP X10 FOR NORMALRV
)@@G@@ RETURN     @E@@@C          SZ        NEGKEY            . CLEAR NEGATIVERW
)@@G@@ KEY  @ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @D@@@C          LMJ       X11,RX
)@@G@@BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@C          TE        A0,NEG,A2       RY
)@@G@@  . IS IT '-'?    @B@@@C          J         $+4               . NO@F@@@CRZ
)@@G@@          SP1       NEGKEY            . YES, SET NEGATIVE KEY     @D@@@CSA
)@@G@@          A         X1,(1,0)          . BUMP CHAR PTR @D@@@C          LMSB
)@@G@@J       X11,BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@C          TNE       A0,ZSC
)@@G@@ERO,A2        . IS IT '0'?    @G@@@C          J         BINTC1          SD
)@@G@@  . YES, GO TO OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC  @E@@@C          L         A0,SBINT  SE
)@@G@@        . NO, RESTORE INPUT A0@E@@@C          TZ        NEGKEY          SF
)@@G@@  . IS NEGATIVE KEY SET?@H@@@C          AN,U      A0,1              . YESG
)@@G@@S, REDUCE # OF CHARS INPUT BY 1     @G@@@C          J         BINTC3    SH
)@@G@@        . GO TO DECIMAL INTEGER LOGIC     @G@@@CBINTC1                  SI
)@@G@@              . OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC FOLLOWS     @E@@@C          DS      SJ
)@@G@@  A3,SBINT+4        . SAVE MORE REGISTERS @ @@@C          S         A5,SSK
)@@G@@BINT+6@G@@@C          L         A3,ZERO,A2        . SET UP LIMITS TO TESSL
)@@G@@T CHARS     @G@@@C          AN,U      A3,1              . CHARS MUST BE SM
)@@G@@BETWEEN 0 AND 7   @A@@@C          L         A4,SEVEN,A2     @F@@@C      SN
)@@G@@    SZ        A5                . BUILD BINARY VALUE IN A5  @F@@@C      SO
)@@G@@    L         A1,SBINT          . INITIALIZE LOOP COUNTER   @^@@@C      SP
)@@G@@    AN,U      A1,1@ @@@C          TZ        NEGKEY    @^@@@C          ANSQ
)@@G@@,U      A1,1@E@@@CBINTL     LMJ       X11,BGET          . GET CHARS 1 BYSR
)@@G@@ 1    @G@@@C          TW        A3,A0             . IS CHAR BETWEEN '0' SS
)@@G@@AND '7'?    @G@@@C          J         BINTC1A           . NO, NOT LEGAL ST
)@@G@@OCTAL INTEGER     @G@@@C          AN        A0,ZERO,A2        . CONVERT SU
)@@G@@CHARACTER TO BINARY     @G@@@C          MSI,U     A5,8              . MUSV
)@@G@@LTIPLY PREVIOUS RESULT BY 8   @D@@@C          A         A5,A0           SW
)@@G@@  . ADD NEW VALUE @D@@@C          A         X1,(1,0)          . BUMP CHASX
)@@G@@R PTR @F@@@C          JGD       A1,BINTL          . IS SCAN OF FIELD COMSY
)@@G@@PLETE?@H@@@C          L         A2,A5             . YES, A5 HAS CONVERTESZ
)@@G@@D OCTAL INTEGER   @ @@@C          J         BINTC2    @G@@@CBINTC1A   ANTA
)@@G@@,U      X10,1             . BAD FORMAT, SETUP FOR BAD RETURN@F@@@CBINTC2TB
)@@G@@    DL        A3,SBINT+4        . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @ @@@C      TC
)@@G@@    L         A5,SBINT+6@F@@@C          J         BINTE             . GOTD
)@@G@@ TO NORMAL EXIT LOGIC   @ @C@B          L         A3,A1     @F@@@CBINTC3TE
)@@G@@    L         A1,X1             . DECIMAL INTEGER LOGIC     @^@C@B      TF
)@@G@@    SZ        A2  @G@C@B          DI,U      A2,6              . CALC WORTG
)@@G@@D # AND BYTE # OF INPUT @ @C@B          LSSL      A3,33     @^@C@B      TH
)@@G@@    LDSL      A2,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A2,0600001@D@@@C          SLTI
)@@G@@J       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @C@B          L         J0,ATJ
)@@G@@2     @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@B          L,U       SR1,TK
)@@G@@0     @ @@@B          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@B          L         A2,ATL
)@@G@@0     @ @@@B          LSSL      A2,27     @ @@@B          L         SR3,TM
)@@G@@A2    @ @C@B          BI        A2,0,X1   @ @@@C          BI        A2,0TN
)@@G@@,*X1  @G@C@B          TZ,H2     SR3               . IF ANY ERROR OCCURRETO
)@@G@@D, A2=0     @F@@@C          TZ,H2     SR3               . IF ANY ERROR OTP
)@@G@@CCURRED,    @^@C@B          L,U       A2,0@E@@@C          AN,U      X10,TQ
)@@G@@1             .   TAKE BAD RETURN   @F@C@B          L         A3,SAVE   TR
)@@G@@        . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @E@@@CBINTE     L         A1,A2     TS
)@@G@@        . IF NEGATIVE KEY SET,@E@@@C          TZ        NEGKEY          TT
)@@G@@  .  SET COMPLEMENT A2  @ @@@C          SN        A1,A2     @F@@@C      TU
)@@G@@    DL        A0,SBINT          . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @ @@@C      TV
)@@G@@    L         X1,SBINT+2@ @@@C          L         X11,X10   @A@@@C      TW
)@@G@@    L         X10,SBINT+3     @C@C@B          J         *BINT           TX
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @C@@@C          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@CTY
)@@G@@.     @H@@@C. **********************************************************TZ
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE BLANK SUBROUTINE                 UA
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           UB
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (UC
)@@G@@BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******   UD
)@@G@@      A0 - # OF BLANKS TO STORE                          *******  @H@@@CUE
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***UF
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BBLANK                  UG
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       UH
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. **********************************UI
)@@G@@****************************************  @]@@@CBBLANK*     @E@@@C      UJ
)@@G@@    DS        A0,SAVE           . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S UK
)@@G@@        A2,SAVE+2 @F@@@C          SPD       A1                . TURN ON UL
)@@G@@CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD     UM
)@@G@@  0,A2@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,XUN
)@@G@@1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@CUO
)@@G@@          L         J0,A1     @^@@@C          AN,U      A0,1@A@@@C      UP
)@@G@@    L         A1,BLANKS,A2    @D@@@C          S,4       A1,0,*X1        UQ
)@@G@@  . STORE BLANKS  @ @@@C          JGD       A0,$-1    @F@@@C          SPUR
)@@G@@D       A1                . TURN OFF CHARACTER MODE   @^@@@C          ANUS
)@@G@@,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@F@@@C          DL        A0,SUT
)@@G@@AVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @ @@@C          L         A2,SUU
)@@G@@AVE+2 @ @@@C          J         0,X11     @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********UV
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@CUW
)@@G@@. ******* BYTE SEARCH SUBROUTINE                                     ***UX
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   UY
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESUZ
)@@G@@S)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - SEARCH BYTE (VA
)@@G@@IF=-BYTE SEARCH NOT EQUAL USED)  *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - #VB
)@@G@@ OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUVC
)@@G@@TPUT: A2 - BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE                          *******  @H@@@CVD
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***VE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BSEARCH                 VF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND          VG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FINDVH
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. *******               VI
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. **********VJ
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @]@@@CVK
)@@G@@BSEARCH*    @E@@@C          DS        A0,SAVE           . SAVE REGISTERSVL
)@@G@@ USED @ @@@C          S         R1,SAVE+2 @F@@@C          SPD       A1  VM
)@@G@@              . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A1,1VN
)@@G@@@^@@@C          LPD       0,A2@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@CVO
)@@G@@          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF           VP
)@@G@@  . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @F@@@C          L VQ
)@@G@@        A1,X1             . CALC # OF BYTES TO SEARCH @ @@@C          SSVR
)@@G@@L       A1,18     @ @@@C          AN        A1,R1     @F@@@C          JPVS
)@@G@@        A1,BSNO           . SKIP SEARCH IF COUNT <=0  @ @@@C          SNVT
)@@G@@        A1,R1     @E@@@C          TN        A0                . IF A0<0,VU
)@@G@@ USE SNE    @E@@@C          J         BSC1              .   OTHERWISE USVV
)@@G@@E SE  @ @@@C          LN        A1,A0     @ @@@C          SNE,4     A1,0VW
)@@G@@,*X1  @^@@@C          J         BSNO@^@@@C          J         BSC2@E@@@CVX
)@@G@@BSC1      SE,4      A0,0,*X1          . SEARCH FOR BYTE     @C@@@C      VY
)@@G@@    J         BSNO              . NO FIND @F@@@CBSC2      L         A1,JVZ
)@@G@@0             . CALC BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE @^@@@C          LXI,U     A1,0WA
)@@G@@@^@@@C          DSL       A1,3@ @@@C          L         A0,BASCII @ @@@CWB
)@@G@@          MSI       A1,NBIT,A0@A@@@C          SSL       A2,*NSHIFT,A0   WC
)@@G@@@ @@@C          A         A2,A1     @^@@@C          AN,U      A2,1@ @@@CWD
)@@G@@          A,U       X11,1     @E@@@CBSNO      SPD       A1              WE
)@@G@@  . CLEAR CHARACTER MODE@^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPWF
)@@G@@D       0,A1@ @@@C          DL        A0,SAVE   @ @@@C          L       WG
)@@G@@  R1,SAVE+2 @C@@@C          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@CWH
)@@G@@.     @H@@@C. **********************************************************WI
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE COMPARE SUBROUTINE               WJ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           WK
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (WL
)@@G@@BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 1)                 *******  @H@@@C. *******   WM
)@@G@@      X2 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 2)                 *******  @H@@@CWN
)@@G@@. *******         A0 - # OF BYTES TO COMPARE                         ***WO
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - 0 IF 2 STRINGS COMPARE               WP
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       WQ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,WR
)@@G@@BCOMP                            *******  @H@@@C. *******               WS
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. **********WT
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@CWU
)@@G@@BCOMP*@E@@@C          DS        A1,SBCOMP         . SAVE REGISTERS USED WV
)@@G@@@A@@@C          S         X2,SBCOMP+2     @A@@@C          S         X1,SWW
)@@G@@BCOMP+3     @A@@@C          S         X11,SBCOMP+4    @ @@@C          L,WX
)@@G@@H1      A2,BASCII @F@@@C          TNE,H2    A2,BASCII         . IS CONVEWY
)@@G@@RSION IMPLIED?    @B@@@C          J         BCOMPC            . NO@G@@@CWZ
)@@G@@          L,U       X2,BUFF           . CONVERT 1ST STRING INTO BUFF    XA
)@@G@@@ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @F@@@C          L         X11,SBCOMPXB
)@@G@@+4      . RESTORE RETURN ADDRESS    @F@@@C          L         X1,X2     XC
)@@G@@        . USE BUFF FOR COMPARISON   @A@@@C          L         X2,SBCOMP+XD
)@@G@@2     @ @@@C          L,H2      A2,BASCII @ @@@CBCOMPC    L         A1,XXE
)@@G@@1     @C@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . SETUP J0@ @@@C      XF
)@@G@@    L         J0,A1     @ @@@C          L         A1,X2     @C@@@C      XG
)@@G@@    SLJ       STUFF             . SETUP J1@ @@@C          L         J1,AXH
)@@G@@1     @ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@C          L,U       SR2,XI
)@@G@@0     @ @@@C          S         A0,A1     @^@@@C          LSSL      A0,9XJ
)@@G@@@ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @ @@@C          LSSL      A0,18     XK
)@@G@@@D@@@C          L         SR3,A0            . SETUP SR3     @D@@@C      XL
)@@G@@    BC        A0,,*X1           . BYTE COMPARE  @F@@@C          DL      XM
)@@G@@  A1,SBCOMP         . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @A@@@C          L       XN
)@@G@@  X1,SBCOMP+3     @C@@@C          J         0,X11             . RETURN  XO
)@@G@@@[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************************************XP

)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - (XU

)@@G@@      R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@@@CXW

)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BYTE # OF START OF FIELD XZ

)@@G@@**********************  @]@@@CGETSFIELD*  @E@@@C          SP1       SFIEZC
)@@G@@LDKEY         . SET SUBFIELD KEY    @E@@@C          S         X11,SAVE+5ZD
