)@@G@@  . BYTE # OF ' ' OR ','@F@@@C          AN        A0,TEMP           . CAZX
)@@G@@LC # OF BYTES TO MOVE   @E@@@C          TG        A0,R2             . CHZY
)@@G@@ECK FOR MAX SIZE  @ @@@C          L         A0,R2     @E@@@D          L ZZ
)@@G@@        A1,BASCII         . RESTORE ASCII KEYS  @ @@@D          SSC     AA
)@@G@@  A1,18     @ @@@D          S         A1,BASCII @E@@@C          LMJ     AB
)@@G@@  X11,BMOVE         . MOVE FIELD TO OUTPUT@D@@@C          L         X11,AC
)@@G@@SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @F@@@C          A,U       X11,1           AD
)@@G@@  . POINT TO NORMAL RETURN    @ @@@C          L         A1,TEMP   @ @@@CAE
)@@G@@          AN        A2,A1     @ @@@C          L         A0,A2     @D@@@CAF
)@@G@@          J         $+2               . NORMAL RETURN @D@@@CGETFE     L AG
)@@G@@        X11,SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@C          L         A2,SAH
)@@G@@AVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+4 @ @@@C          L         X3,SAI
)@@G@@AVE+6 @C@@@C          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     AJ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************AK
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@C. ******* FIND GIVEN FIELD SUBROUTINE                 AL
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 AM
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #AN
)@@G@@,BASE ADDRESS OF BLOCK)                *******  @H@@@C. *******         AO
)@@G@@X2 - (BYTE #,BASE ADDRESS OF FIELD)                *******  @H@@@C. ****AP
)@@G@@***         A1 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN BLOCK                      *******  AQ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******         A2 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN FIELD                   AR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE # IN BLOCK WHERE FIELD FOUAS
)@@G@@ND             *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 AT
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMAU
)@@G@@J X11,FINDFIELD                        *******  @H@@@C. *******         AV
)@@G@@            J NOFIND                               *******  @H@@@C. ****AW
)@@G@@***                     J FIND                                 *******  AX
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                                                         AY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ****************************************************AZ
)@@G@@**********************  @]@@@CFINDFIELD*  @E@@@C          S         X11,BA
)@@G@@SAVE+2        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          DS        A1,SAVE+3 BB
)@@G@@@ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+5 @H@@@C          AN        A1,A2     BC
)@@G@@        . CALC # OF TIMES TO COMPARE FIELDS     @ @@@C          S       BD
)@@G@@  A1,R1     @ @@@C          L         A0,A2     @E@@@C          LMJ     BE
)@@G@@  X11,BCOMP         . COMPARE 2 FIELDS    @D@@@C          JZ        A0,FBF
)@@G@@INDF          . FIELD FOUND   @E@@@C          A         X1,(1,0)        BG
)@@G@@  . BUMP BYTE # OF BLOCK@F@@@C          JGD       R1,$-4            . CHBH
)@@G@@ECK FOR END OF BLOCK    @G@@@C          J         FINDN             . ENBI
)@@G@@D OF BLOCK, FIELD NOT FOUND   @G@@@CFINDF     L         A0,X1           BJ
)@@G@@  . GET BYTE # WHERE FIELD FOUND    @ @@@C          SSL       A0,18     BK
)@@G@@@D@@@C          L         X11,SAVE+2        . RESTORE X11   @F@@@C      BL
)@@G@@    A,U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAL RETURN    @D@@@C      BM
)@@G@@    J         $+2               . NORMAL RETURN @D@@@CFINDN     L       BN
)@@G@@  X11,SAVE+2        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@C          DL        A1,SAVE+3 BO
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+5 @C@@@C          J         0,X11     BP
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************BQ
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@C. ******* CONVERT TIME/DBR
)@@G@@ATE STRING TO TDATE$ FORMAT SUBROUTINE       *******  @H@@@C. ******* (SBS
)@@G@@TRINGS CAN BE OF FORM: 'HH:MM:SS' OR 'MM/DD/YY')         *******  @H@@@CBT
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***BU
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)          BV
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRINBW
)@@G@@G                    *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - TDATE$ WORD  BX
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BBY
)@@G@@YTE # AFTER FIELD                            *******  @H@@@C. *******   BZ
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CCA
)@@G@@. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BTDATE                           ***CB
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                     J ERROR                       CC
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J NORMAL          CD
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           CE
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. **********************CF
)@@G@@****************************************************  @]@@@CBTDATE*     CG
)@@G@@@E@@@C          S         X11,10            . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@CCH
)@@G@@          S         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@C          DS        A1,SBTDATE+1    CI
)@@G@@@A@@@C          S         X2,SBTDATE+3    @A@@@C          S         A3,SCJ
)@@G@@BTDATE+4    @D@@@C          L         A0,BASCII         . ASCII KEY     CK
)@@G@@@G@@@C          LSSL      A0,18             . SHIFT H1 TO H2 FOR GETFIELCL
)@@G@@D     @ @@@C          S         A0,BASCII @D@@@C          SZ        TDATCM
)@@G@@EA            . CLEAR OUTPUT  @E@@@C          L,U       X2,BUFF         CN
)@@G@@  . EXTRACT NEXT FIELD  @^@@@C          L,U       R2,8@A@@@C          LMCO
)@@G@@J       X11,GETFIELD    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NOCP
)@@G@@ MORE FIELDS@F@@@C          A         A0,A1             . CALC BYTE # AFCQ
)@@G@@TER FIELD   @C@@@C          S         A0,SBTDATE+1      . SAVE    @F@@@CCR
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,'/'            . IS FIELD DATE OR TIME?    @ @@@CCS
)@@G@@          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @C@@@C          J         TDATET          CT
)@@G@@  . TIME    @D@@@C          TE,S6     A0,BUFF           . CHECK FORMAT  CU
)@@G@@@D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @^@@@C      CV
)@@G@@    L,U       A2,0@ @@@C          L,U       A3,12     @D@@@C          L,CW
)@@G@@S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'CX
)@@G@@0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BCY
)@@G@@UFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,ACZ
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMIDA
)@@G@@TS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@CDB
)@@G@@          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C      DC
)@@G@@    L,U       A3,31     @D@@@C          L,S4      A0,BUFF           . CODD
)@@G@@NVERT 'DD'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U   DE
)@@G@@  A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U    DF
)@@G@@  A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW      DG
)@@G@@  A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J       DH
)@@G@@  BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S2      A0,TDATEA DI
)@@G@@        . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,U       A2,64     @ @@@CDJ
)@@G@@          L,U       A3,99     @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF+1       DK
)@@G@@  . CONVERT 'YY'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSDL
)@@G@@I,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BUFF+1 @ @@@C          ANDM
)@@G@@,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TWDN
)@@G@@        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J DO
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @D@@@C          AN,U      A0,6DP
)@@G@@4             . MODULO 64     @E@@@C          S,S3      A0,TDATEA       DQ
)@@G@@  . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L         A0,TDATEA         . GEDR
)@@G@@T OUTPUT    @C@@@C          J         BTDATEE           . RETURN  @F@@@CDS
)@@G@@TDATET    L,U       A0,':'            . CHECK FOR FORMAT ERROR    @ @@@CDT
)@@G@@          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1       DU
)@@G@@  . FORMAT ERROR  @ @@@C          TE,S6     A0,BUFF   @D@@@C          J DV
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @^@@@C          LN,U      A2,1DW
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L,U       A3,23     @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF   DX
)@@G@@        . CONVERT 'HH'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C      DY
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C      DZ
)@@G@@    AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C      EA
)@@G@@    TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C      EB
)@@G@@    J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S1    EC
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,U       A3,5ED
)@@G@@9     @D@@@C          L,S4      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@CEE
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@CEF
)@@G@@          L,S5      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@CEG
)@@G@@          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0           EH
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1       EI
)@@G@@  . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S2      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOEJ
)@@G@@R OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF+1         . CONVERT 'SS'  EK
)@@G@@@ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     EL
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BUFF+1 @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    EM
)@@G@@@ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0     EN
)@@G@@        . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1 EO
)@@G@@        . NO, ERROR     @ @@@C          S,S3      A0,TDATEA @H@@@C      EP
)@@G@@    L,S1      A0,TDATEA         . CONVERT HH,MM,SS TO SECS PAST MIDNIGHTEQ
)@@G@@@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C          A,S2      A0,TDATEA ER
)@@G@@@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C          A,S3      A0,TDATEA ES
)@@G@@@F@@@CBTDATEE   A,U       X10,1             . POINT TO NORMAL RETURN    ET
)@@G@@@G@@@C          L         A1,BASCII         . RESTORE BASCII TO ORIGINALEU
)@@G@@ VALUE@ @@@C          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@C          S         A1,BEV
)@@G@@ASCII @ @@@C          L         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@C          DL        A1,SEW
)@@G@@BTDATE+1    @A@@@C          L         X2,SBTDATE+3    @A@@@C          L EX
)@@G@@        A3,SBTDATE+4    @C@@@C          J         0,X10             . REEY
)@@G@@TURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************************EZ
)@@G@@****************************  @H@@@C. ******* EXTRACT FILE NAME STRING SFA
)@@G@@UBROUTINE                        *******  @H@@@C. *******               FB
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* INFC
)@@G@@PUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@CFD
)@@G@@. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    ***FE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - OUTPUT BUFFER                        FF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: OUT,+1  - QUALIFIER           FG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******         OUT+2,3 - FILE-NAMFH
)@@G@@E                                *******  @H@@@C. *******         OUT+4 FI
)@@G@@  - CYCLE (OCTAL)                            *******  @H@@@C. *******   FJ
)@@G@@      A0 = # OF BYTES IN FIELD                           *******  @H@@@CFK
)@@G@@. *******         A1 = BYTE # OF START OF FIELD                      ***FL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   FM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BFILE       FN
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J ERROFO
)@@G@@R                                *******  @H@@@C. *******               FP
)@@G@@      J NORMAL                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   FQ
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CFR
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************FS
)@@G@@****  @[@@@CBFILE*@E@@@C          S         X11,X10           . SAVE REGFT
)@@G@@ISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBFILE @A@@@C          S       FU
)@@G@@  X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          S         X3,SBFILE+2     @A@@@C      FV
)@@G@@    DS        A2,SBFILE+6     @E@@@C          L,U       X2,BUFF         FW
)@@G@@  . FIND LIMITS OF FIELD@ @@@C          L,U       R2,46     @A@@@C      FX
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @F@@@C          J         BFILEE+1        FY
)@@G@@  . NO FIELD FOUND, ERROR     @F@@@C          DS        A0,SBFILE+4     FZ
)@@G@@  . SAVE GETFIELD OUTPUTS     @E@@@C          A         A0,A1           GA
)@@G@@  . CALC END BYTE #     @C@@@C          S         A0,SBFILE+3       . SAGB
)@@G@@VE    @ @@@C          LXI       X1,A1     @F@@@C          L         A3,AGC
)@@G@@1             . A3 = CURRENT BYTE POINTER @D@@@C          L         X2,SGD
)@@G@@BFILE+1       . RESTORE X2    @D@@@C          L,H1      X3,BASCII       GE
)@@G@@  . ASCII KEY     @E@@@C          L         A0,BLANKS,X3      . INITIALIGF
)@@G@@ZE OUTPUT   @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     @ @@@C          DS      GG
)@@G@@  A0,0,X2   @ @@@C          DS        A0,2,X2   @^@@@C          SZ      GH
)@@G@@  4,X2@D@@@C          L         A0,ASTER,X3       . SEARCH FOR '*'@A@@@CGI
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @D@@@C          SZ        A2        GJ
)@@G@@        . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C          S         A2,QUALKEY        . SAGK
)@@G@@VE BYTE # OF '*'  @D@@@C          L         A0,LPAREN,X3      . SEARCH FGL
)@@G@@OR '('@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @D@@@C          SZ      GM
)@@G@@  A2                . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C          S         A2,CYCLEKEGN
)@@G@@Y       . SAVE BYTE # OF '('  @F@@@C          L         A0,QUALKEY      GO
)@@G@@  . IS THERE A QUALIFIER?     @B@@@C          JZ        A0,BFILEC       GP
)@@G@@  . NO@G@@@C          AN        A0,A3             . CALC SIZE OF QUALIFIGQ
)@@G@@ER SUBFIELD @F@@@C          LXI,U     X2,0              . MOVE QUALIFIERGR
)@@G@@ TO OUTPUT  @ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @E@@@C          L       GS
)@@G@@  A3,QUALKEY        . BUMP A3 PAST '*'    @^@@@C          A,U       A3,1GT
)@@G@@@ @@@C          LXI       X1,A3     @E@@@CBFILEC    L         A0,CYCLEKEGU
)@@G@@Y       . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @^@@@C          TNZ       A0  @E@@@C      GV
)@@G@@    L         A0,SBFILE+3       . NO, USE END BYTE #  @H@@@C          ANGW
)@@G@@        A0,A3             .   TO CALCULATE SIZE OF FILE FIELD     @ @@@CGX
)@@G@@          LXI,U     X2,12     @F@@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE       GY
)@@G@@  . MOVE FILE-NAME TO OUTPUT  @F@@@C          A,U       A3,1,A0         GZ
)@@G@@  . BUMP A3 PAST FILE-NAME    @E@@@C          TNZ       CYCLEKEY        HA
)@@G@@  . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @D@@@C          J         BFILEE            . NOHB
)@@G@@, FINISHED  @F@@@C          LXI       X1,A3             . PREPARE TO EXTHC
)@@G@@RACT CYCLE  @A@@@C          AN        A3,SBFILE+3     @ @@@C          LNHD
)@@G@@,XU     A0,1,A3   @F@@@C          LMJ       X11,BINT          . CONVERT HE
)@@G@@CYCLE TO BINARY   @D@@@C          J         BFILEE+1          . FORMAT EHF
)@@G@@RROR  @F@@@C          S         A2,4,X2           . STORE CYCLE IN OUTPUHG
)@@G@@T     @G@@@CBFILEE    A,U       X10,1             . GENERATE NORMAL RETUHH
)@@G@@RN ADDRESS  @ @@@C          L         X1,SBFILE @A@@@C          L       HI
)@@G@@  X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          L         X3,SBFILE+2     @A@@@C      HJ
)@@G@@    DL        A0,SBFILE+4     @A@@@C          DL        A2,SBFILE+6     HK
)@@G@@@C@@@C          J         0,X10             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@CHL
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************HM
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* J-REG STUFF LOCAL SUBROUTINE                      HN
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       HO
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT: A1 = (BYTE #,X)    HP
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. *******        A2 = ASHQ
)@@G@@CII KEY                                      *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUHR
)@@G@@TPUT: A1 = CORRESPONDING J-REG                           *******  @H@@@CHS
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***HT
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. **********************************************************HU
)@@G@@****************  @^@@@CSTUFF     +         0   @D@@@C          DS      HV
)@@G@@  A2,STUFFD         . SAVE A2,A3    @ @@@C          L         A3,A2     HW
)@@G@@@ @@@C          DSL       A1,54     @ @@@C          JZ        A2,STUFFC HX
)@@G@@@ @@@C          DI        A1,NBIT,A3@A@@@C          LSSL      A2,*NSHIFTHY
)@@G@@,A3   @^@@@C          LDSL      A1,3@D@@@CSTUFFC    LXI       A1,UJ0,A3 HZ
)@@G@@        . SET UPPER JO  @D@@@C          DL        A2,STUFFD         . REIA
)@@G@@STORE A2,A3 @ @@@C          J         *STUFF    @H@@@C. ****************IB
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @^@C@BSAVE  IC
)@@G@@    RES       2   @[@@@C$(0)  @H@@@CBASCII*   +         0               ID
)@@G@@  . ASCII KEY (INITIALLY OFF FOR FIELDATA)@^@@@CSTUFFD    $RES      2   IE
)@@G@@@^@@@CNBIT      +         6   @^@@@C          +         4   @^@@@CNSHIFTIF
)@@G@@    +         33  @^@@@C          +         34  @ @@@CUJ0       +       IG
)@@G@@  0600001   @ @@@C          +         0400002   @ @@@CCONVT     +       IH
)@@G@@  FDASCT    @ @@@C          +         ASCFDT    @ @@@CBMOVET    BM      II
)@@G@@  0,*X1     @ @@@C          BMT       0,*X1     @#@@@CBLANKS    '      'IJ
)@@G@@@^@@@C          $CAS('    ')  @^@@@CSPACE     +         ' ' @ @@@C      IK
)@@G@@    +         $CAS(' ') @^@@@CCOMMA     +         ',' @ @@@C          + IL
)@@G@@        $CAS(',') @^@@@CNEG       +         '-' @ @@@C          +       IM
)@@G@@  $CAS('-') @^@@@CZERO      +         '0' @ @@@C          +         $CASIN
)@@G@@('0') @^@@@CSEVEN     +         '7' @ @@@C          +         $CAS('7') IO
)@@G@@@^@@@CSLASH     +         '/' @ @@@C          +         $CAS('/') @^@@@CIP
)@@G@@COLON     +         ':' @ @@@C          +         $CAS(':') @^@@@CASTER IQ
)@@G@@    +         '*' @ @@@C          +         $CAS('*') @^@@@CLPAREN    + IR
)@@G@@        '(' @ @@@C          +         $CAS('(') @^@@@CRPAREN    +       IS
)@@G@@  ')' @ @@@C          +         $CAS(')') @^@@@CSAVE      $RES      7   IT
)@@G@@@^@@@CSBCOMP    $RES      5   @^@@@CSBMOVE    $RES      3   @^@@@CSBGET IU
)@@G@@    $RES      2   @^@@@CSBTDATE   $RES      6   @^@@@CSBFILE    $RES    IV
)@@G@@  7   @^@@@CSBINT     $RES      7   @^@@@CNEGKEY    $RES      1   @^@@@CIW
)@@G@@QUALKEY   $RES      1   @^@@@CCYCLEKEY  $RES      1   @^@@@CSFIELDKEY $RIX
)@@G@@ES      1   @^@@@CTEMP      $RES      1   @^@@@CTDATEA    $RES      1   IY
)@@G@@@#@@@CFDASCT    $ASCII  @H@@@C          '@[]#  ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYIZ
)@@G@@Z)-+<=>&$*(%:?!,\0123456789'';/." ' @#@@@CASCFDT    $FDATA  @ @@@C $DO 8JA
)@@G@@ ,  ' ',' ',' ',' '     @ @@@C          ' ','!','"','#'     @ @@@C      JB
)@@G@@    '$','%','&',''''    @ @@@C          '(',')','*','+'     @ @@@C      JC
)@@G@@    ',','_','.','/'     @ @@@C          '0','1','2','3'     @ @@@C      JD
)@@G@@    '4','5','6','7'     @ @@@C          '8','9',':',';'     @ @@@C      JE
)@@G@@    '<','=','>','?'     @ @@@C          '@','A','B','C'     @ @@@C      JF
)@@G@@    'D','E','F','G'     @ @@@C          'H','I','J','K'     @ @@@C      JG
)@@G@@    'L','M','N','O'     @ @@@C          'P','Q','R','S'     @ @@@C      JH
)@@G@@    'T','U','V','W'     @ @@@C          'X','Y','Z','['     @ @@@C      JI
)@@G@@    '\',']','^','_'     @ @@@C          ' ','A','B','C'     @ @@@C      JJ
)@@G@@    'D','E','F','G'     @ @@@C          'H','I','J','K'     @ @@@C      JK
)@@G@@    'L','M','N','O'     @ @@@C          'P','Q','R','S'     @ @@@C      JL
)@@G@@    'T','U','V','W'     @ @@@C          'X','Y','Z',' '     @ @@@C      JM
)@@G@@    ' ',' ',' ',' '     @^@@@CBUFF      $RES      50  @#@@@C          $EJN
)@@G@@ND    ___     X2,0              . MOVE QUALIFIER)@@[F#@[#@[#@@K[#@@K@@@@JO

)@@G@@    LMJ       X7,EDFD1          . EDIT IT @C@@@@          J         ENDTDI
)@@G@@6             . TO EXIT @]@@@@EDHEXRT.    @C@@@@ . THIS ROUTINE PERFORMSDJ
)@@G@@ HEXADECIMAL EDITING .  @G@@@@ . IT TAKES A QUARTER WORD AND DROPS THE HDK
)@@G@@IGHEST ORDER BIT. REST OF     @H@@@@ . 8 BITS ARE EDITED IN TWO HEX DIGIDL
)@@G@@TS , THUS EDITING ONE WORD IN 8 HEX DIGITS@D@@@@          L         X6,(DM
)@@G@@1,0)          . SET REG X6    @H@@@@          L,U       A5,3            DN
)@@G@@  . JGD CNT TO MANIPULATE 4 QTR. WRDS     @B@@@@BACK2     LSSL      A1,1DO
)@@G@@              .   @H@@@@          L,U       A6,1              . JGD CNT DP
)@@G@@TO GET 2 CHARS PER QTR WRD    @B@@@@BACK1     LSSC      A1,4            DQ
)@@G@@  .   @B@@@@          DSL       A1,4              .   @B@@@@          LSDR
)@@G@@SL      A1,4              .   @B@@@@          SSL       A2,32           DS

)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          JGD       A6,BACK1          .   @B@@@@      DV
)@@G@@    JGD       A5,BACK2          .   @B@@@@          J         0,X10     DW
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@STOR      S,S1      A4,TEMPR          .   @B@@@@      DX
)@@G@@    S,S2      A4,TEMPR          .   @B@@@@          S,S3      A4,TEMPR  DY
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          S,S4      A4,TEMPR          .   @B@@@@      DZ
)@@G@@    S,S5      A4,TEMPR          .   @B@@@@          S,S6      A4,TEMPR  EA
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          S,S1      A4,TEMPR+1        .   @B@@@@      EB
)@@G@@    S,S2      A4,TEMPR+1        .   @]@@@@EDNONSNS.   @H@@@@          . EC
)@@G@@THIS EDITS THE LOG ENTRY IN NONSENSE INTERRUPT LOG BUFFER FORMAT  @E@@@@ED
)@@G@@          L,U       A11,T6NWNOI       . GET # OF INTERRUPTS @B@@@@      EE
)@@G@@    L,S2      A14,1,X2          .   @E@@@@          L         A6,A14    EF

)@@G@@IS PROGRAM WILL ALLOW SELECTIVE PRINTING/DUMPING         *******  @H@@@IFV
)@@G@@. ******* OF ENTRIES IN THE SYSTEM LOG OR LOG TAPE.                  ***FW
)@@G@@****  @H@@@I. *******                                                   FX
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: @LOGDUMP[,OPTIONS]  FY
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@I. *******                           FZ
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@I. ******* THE FOLLOWING GA
)@@G@@DATA CARD FORMATS ARE RECOGNIZED:            *******  @H@@@I. *******   GB
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@IGC
)@@G@@. ******* TYPE N,N,...,N - PRINT LOG TYPES N,N,...,N                 ***GD
)@@G@@****  @H@@@I. ******* DUMP N,N,...,N - DUMP  LOG TYPES N,N,...,N        GE
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. ******* RUNID N,N,..,N - PROCESS ONLY LOGS FORGF
)@@G@@ RUNIDS N,N,..,N     *******  @H@@@I. ******* TIME MM/DD/YY HH:MM:SS TO GG
)@@G@@MM/DD/YY HH:MM:SS                *******  @H@@@J. ******* TEST WORD,VALUGH
)@@G@@E ... WORD,VALUE - TEST SPECIFIC WORDS FOR   *******  @H@@@J. *******   GI
)@@G@@                               FOR SPECIFIC VALUES       *******  @H@@@JGJ
)@@G@@. ******* FILE Q*F,Q*F,...,Q*F - FOR TYPE 3 LOGS, PROCESS ONLY       ***GK
)@@G@@****  @H@@@J. *******                        THOSE FOR SPECIFIED FILES  GL
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. *******                                       GM
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@I. ******* THE RUNID FEATURE INCLUDESGN
)@@G@@ SCANNING OF LOG ENTRIES WHICH   *******  @H@@@I. ******* ARE NOT DIRECTGO
)@@G@@LY RELATED TO THE RUNIDS BUT MAY CONTAIN     *******  @H@@@I. ******* A GP
)@@G@@REFERENCE TO THE RUNIDS.  FOR EXAMPLE, EXEC LOG ENTRIES  *******  @H@@@IGQ
)@@G@@. ******* MAY INCLUDE CONSOLE MESSAGES WHICH CONTAIN THE RUNID.      ***GR
)@@G@@****  @H@@@I. *******                                                   GS
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. ******* IF NO TYPE OR DUMP DATA CARDS ARE ENCOGT
)@@G@@UNTERED, ALL LOG     *******  @H@@@I. ******* ENTRIES ARE SCANNED (EXCEPGU
)@@G@@T EXEC LOG ENTRIES).  HOWEVER,   *******  @H@@@I. ******* IF TYPE OR DUMGV
)@@G@@P DATA CARDS ARE ENCOUNTERED, ONLY THE LOG   *******  @H@@@I. ******* ENGW
)@@G@@TRY TYPES SPECIFIED ON THOSE CARDS WILL BE SCANNED.      *******  @H@@@KGX
)@@G@@. ******* THE ONE EXCEPTION TO THIS RULE IS IF A 'DUMP ALL' CARD     ***GY
)@@G@@****  @H@@@K. ******* IS ENCOUNTERED, ALL LOG ENTRIES WHICH ARE TO BE EDGZ
)@@G@@ITTED    *******  @H@@@K. ******* WILL ALSO BE DUMPED.                  HA
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@I. *******                           HB
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@I. ******* ONLY PRIVILEGEHC
)@@G@@D RUNS ARE ALLOWED ACCESS TO EXEC LOG        *******  @H@@@I. ******* ENHD
)@@G@@TRIES.                                                   *******  @H@@@IHE
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***HF
)@@G@@****  @H@@@I. ******* IF 'L' OPTION SPECIFIED, SYSTEM LOG CYCLE INFORMATHG
)@@G@@ION      *******  @H@@@I. ******* WILL BE PRINTED.  IF A FILE 'LOG$' IS HH
)@@G@@ASSIGNED TO RUN,     *******  @H@@@I. ******* IT WILL BE READ INSTEAD OFHI
)@@G@@ SYSTEM LOG.                     *******  @H@@@J. *******               HJ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@J. ******* IFHK
)@@G@@ 'N' OPTION SPECIFIED, THE LOG ENTRIES WILL BE PRINTED   *******  @H@@@JHL
)@@G@@. ******* IN AN ABBREVIATED 1 LINE FORMAT.  DUMP FORMATS ARE NOT     ***HM
)@@G@@****  @H@@@J. ******* AFFECTED.                                         HN
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. *******                                       HO
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@J@I. ******* PROGRAM USES 'READLG', 'BYHP
)@@G@@TESUB', AND 'GUESS' SUBROUTINES. *******  @H@@@J. ******* PROGRAM USES 'HQ
)@@G@@READLG' AND 'BYTESUB' SUBROUTINES.           *******  @H@@@I. ******* PRHR
)@@G@@OGRAM ALSO USES 'LOGFED' AS A SUBROUTINE TO FORMAT       *******  @H@@@IHS

)@@G@@C     @F@@@J          L         X8,(28,BUFF)      . INITIALIZE FOR LOGFEVP
)@@G@@D     @ @@@I          L,U       X5,100000 @F@@@I          J         LOGFVQ
)@@G@@ED            . LET LOGFED DO ALL THE WORK@[@@@J.     @F@@@J. **********VR

)@@G@@24, PRINT SUBTYPE ALSO  @ @@@J          TE,S1     A0,BUFF   @ @@@J      VY

)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@J@I. *******   XF
)@@G@@        GET NEXT SUBFIELD FROM CARD IMAGE                *******  @H@J@IXG
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***XH
)@@G@@****  @H@J@I. ******* INPUT - X1 = (BYTE,IMAGE)                         XI
)@@G@@         *******  @H@J@I. ******* OUTPUT - A2 = NEXT ENTRY TYPE (IF 'NEXXJ
)@@G@@TINT' CALLED)        *******  @H@J@I. *******             = NEXT SUBFIELXK
)@@G@@D (IF 'NEXTFIELD' CALLED)        *******  @H@J@I. *******               XL
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@J@I. **********XM
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @G@J@IXN
)@@G@@NEXTINT   L,U       A7,0              . GET NEXT INTEGER SUBFIELD ENTRY XO
)@@G@@@^@J@I          J         $+2 @F@J@INEXTFIELD L,U       A7,1            XP
)@@G@@  . GET NEXT SUBFIELD ENTRY   @H@J@I          L         A0,X1           XQ
)@@G@@  . CALCULATE # OF CHARS LEFT IN INPUT    @ @J@I          SSL       A0,1XR
)@@G@@8     @ @J@I          AN        A0,INCHARS@G@J@I          JP        A0,0XS
)@@G@@,X10          . NO CHARS LEFT, FINISHED IMAGE   @ @J@I          SN      XT
)@@G@@  A0,R1     @ @J@I          LN,U      A0,' '    @F@J@I          LMJ     XU
)@@G@@  X11,BSEARCH       . FIND NEXT NON-BLANK CHAR  @E@J@I          J       XV
)@@G@@  0,X10             . FINISHED INPUT IMAGE@F@J@I          LXI       X1,AXW
)@@G@@2             . UPDATE X1 TO NON-BLANK POS@F@J@I          AN        A2,IXX
)@@G@@NCHARS        . CALCULATE # OF CHARS LEFT @ @J@I          SN        A2,RXY
)@@G@@1     @ @J@I          L,U       A0,','    @E@J@I          LMJ       X11,XZ
)@@G@@BSEARCH       . FIND NEXT ',' IF ANY@F@J@I          J         $+2       YA
)@@G@@        . NO COMMA, LOOK FOR BLANK  @ @J@I          J         NEXTC     YB
)@@G@@@ @J@I          L,U       A0,' '    @A@J@I          LMJ       X11,BSEARCYC
)@@G@@H     @H@J@I          L         A2,INCHARS        . SUBFIELD IN LAST POSYD
)@@G@@ITIONS OF IMAGE   @F@J@INEXTC     L         A5,X1             . CALCULATYE
)@@G@@E SIZE OF SUBFIELD@ @J@I          SSL       A5,18     @ @J@I          ANYF
)@@G@@        A2,A5     @ @J@I          L         A0,A2     @ @J@I          L,YG
)@@G@@U       X2,FIELD2 @E@J@I          SFS       FIELD2            . BLANK OUYH
)@@G@@T FIELD2    @G@J@I          TNZ       A7                . IF 'NEXTFIELD'YI
)@@G@@ ENTRY, CALL BMOVE@^@J@I          J         $+4 @ @J@I          LMJ     YJ
)@@G@@  X11,BMOVE @ @J@I          L         A2,FIELD2 @^@J@I          J       YK
)@@G@@  $+2 @G@J@I          LMJ       X11,BINT          . IF 'NEXTINT' ENTRY, YL
)@@G@@CALL BINT   @H@J@I          A,U       A5,1,A0           . UPDATE X1 WITHYM
)@@G@@ SIZE OF SUBFIELD+1     @ @J@I          LXI       X1,A5     @C@J@I      YN
)@@G@@    J         1,X10             . RETURN  @H@@@I. **********************YO
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@J@I. *******   YP
)@@G@@        ADD ENTRY TYPE TO TABLE                          *******  @H@@@JYQ
)@@G@@. *******           ADD ENTRY TO TABLE SUBROUTINE                    ***YR
)@@G@@****  @H@@@I. *******                                                   YS
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@I. ******* INPUT - A0 = TABLE POINTER            YT
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@J@I. ******          A2 = ENTRY TYPE   YU
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@J. ******          A2 = EYV
)@@G@@NTRY                                         *******  @H@@@I. *******   YW
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@IYX
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************YY
)@@G@@****  @]@@@IADD       . @F@@@I          L,H1      A1,0,A0           . # YZ
)@@G@@OF ENTRIES IN TABLE     @F@@@I          A,H2      A1,0,A0           . CAZA
)@@G@@LC NEXT AVAILABLE SLOT  @F@J@I          S         A2,0,A1           . STZB
)@@G@@ORE ENTRY TYPE THERE    @E@@@J          S         A2,0,A1           . STZC
)@@G@@ORE ENTRY THERE   @G@@@I          INC,H1    0,A0              . INCREMENZD
)@@G@@T # OF ENTRIES IN TABLE @#@@@I          NOP     @C@@@I          J       ZE
)@@G@@  0,X10             . RETURN  @H@@@J. **********************************ZF
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@J. *******               ZG
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@J. ******* GUZH
)@@G@@ESS WHETHER WORD IN A0 IS TDATE$ FORMAT, INTEGER,        *******  @H@@@JZI
)@@G@@. ******* OR JUST FIELDATA STRING.                                   ***ZJ
)@@G@@****  @H@@@J. *******                                                   ZK
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@J. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: SLJ GUESS           ZL
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@J. *******                           ZM
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@J. ******* INPUT: A0 - INZN
)@@G@@PUT WORD                                     *******  @H@@@J. *******   ZO
)@@G@@     R2 - PRESENT DATE IN TDATE$ FORMAT                  *******  @H@@@JZP
)@@G@@. *******             (PRE-SET AT @XQT TIME)                         ***ZQ
)@@G@@****  @H@@@J. ******                                                    ZR
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@J. **********************************************ZS
)@@G@@****************************  @^@@@JGUESS     +         0   @D@@@J      ZT
)@@G@@    S         A0,INPUT          . SAVE INPUT    @G@@@J          JN      ZU
)@@G@@  A0,STRING         . IF < 0, ASSUME FIELDATA STRING  @ @@@J          TGZV
)@@G@@,U      A0,0400000@^@@@J          J         $+3 @G@@@J          E$DECV  ZW
)@@G@@                    . ASSUME INTEGER IF < 0400000     @ @@@J          J ZX
)@@G@@        *GUESS    @E@@@J          L         A1,R2             . GET PRESZY
)@@G@@ENT DATE    @F@@@J          TLE       A1,INPUT          . IS INPUT > PREZZ
)@@G@@SENT DATE?  @G@@@J          J         STRING            . YES, ASSUME NOAA
)@@G@@T TDATE$ FORMAT   @F@@@J          L,U       A1,0              . CHECK FOAB
)@@G@@R TDATE$ FORMAT   @ @@@J          L,U       A2,12     @ @@@J          TWAC
)@@G@@,S1     A1,INPUT  @B@@@J          J         STRING            . NO@ @@@JAD
)@@G@@          L,U       A2,31     @ @@@J          TW,S2     A1,INPUT  @B@@@JAE
)@@G@@          J         STRING            . NO@ @@@J          L         A1,RAF
)@@G@@2     @ @@@J          LSSL      A1,12     @ @@@J          SSL       A1,3AG
)@@G@@0     @F@@@J          TE,S3     A1,INPUT          . IS YEAR PRESENT YEARAH
)@@G@@?     @B@@@J          J         STRING            . NO@F@@@J          E$AI
)@@G@@DAY1                      . LOOKS LIKE TDATE$ FORMAT  @^@@@J          E$AJ
)@@G@@SKIP    1   @ @@@J          E$TIME    INPUT     @ @@@J          J       AK
)@@G@@  *GUESS    @ @@@JSTRING    E$COPY    6,INPUT   @ @@@J          J       AL
)@@G@@  *GUESS    @^@@@JINPUT     $RES      1   @H@J@I. **********************AM
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@J@I. *******   AN
)@@G@@        CONVERT TO TDATE$ SUBROUTINE                     *******  @H@J@IAO
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***AP
)@@G@@****  @H@J@I. ******* INPUT: X1,X2,R1,R2 - SET FOR GETFIELD             AQ
)@@G@@         *******  @H@J@I. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - DATE OR TIME IN TDATE$ FOAR
)@@G@@RMAT                 *******  @H@J@I. *******         DATEKEY - SET IF DAS
)@@G@@ATE                              *******  @H@J@I. *******         X1,R1 AT
)@@G@@- UPDATED                                    *******  @H@J@I. *******   AU
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@J@IAV
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************AW
)@@G@@****  @]@J@ITDATESUB  . @D@J@I          SZ        DATEKEY           . CLAX
)@@G@@EAR DATE KEY@D@J@I          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD      . GET NEXT FIELDAY
)@@G@@@D@J@I          J         0,X10             . NO MORE FIELDS@D@J@I      AZ
)@@G@@    LXI       X1,A1             . UPDATE X1,R1  @ @J@I          AN      BA
)@@G@@  A1,INCHARS@ @J@I          SN        A1,R1     @F@J@I          L,U     BB
)@@G@@  A0,'/'            . IS FIELD DATE OR TIME?    @ @J@I          TE,S3   BC
)@@G@@  A0,FIELD1 @C@J@I          J         TDATET            . TIME    @D@J@IBD
)@@G@@          TE,S6     A0,FIELD1         . CHECK FORMAT  @D@J@I          J BE
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FORMAT ERROR  @^@J@I          L,U       A2,0BF
)@@G@@@ @J@I          L,U       A3,12     @D@J@I          S         A3,DATEKEYBG
)@@G@@        . SET DATE KEY  @D@J@I          L,S1      A0,FIELD1         . COBH
)@@G@@NVERT 'MM'  @ @J@I          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @J@I          MSI,U   BI
)@@G@@  A0,10     @ @J@I          L,S2      A1,FIELD1 @ @J@I          AN,U    BJ
)@@G@@  A1,'0'    @ @J@I          A         A0,A1     @F@J@I          TW      BK
)@@G@@  A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@J@I          J       BL
)@@G@@  0,X10             . NO, ERROR     @E@J@I          S,S1      A0,TDATEA BM
)@@G@@        . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @J@I          L,U       A3,31     @D@J@IBN
)@@G@@          L,S4      A0,FIELD1         . CONVERT 'DD'  @ @J@I          ANBO
)@@G@@,U      A0,'0'    @ @J@I          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @J@I          L,BP
)@@G@@S5      A1,FIELD1 @ @J@I          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @J@I          A BQ
)@@G@@        A0,A1     @F@J@I          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IFBR
)@@G@@ WITHIN LIMITS    @D@J@I          J         0,X10             . NO, ERROBS
)@@G@@R     @E@J@I          S,S2      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    BT
)@@G@@@ @J@I          L,U       A2,64     @ @J@I          L,U       A3,99     BU

)@@G@@          A         A0,A1     @F@J@I          TW        A2,A0           BY
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@J@I          J         0,X10           BZ
)@@G@@  . NO, ERROR     @D@J@I          AN,U      A0,64             . MODULO 6CA
)@@G@@4     @E@J@I          S,S3      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    CB
)@@G@@@ @J@I          L,H1      A0,TDATEA @C@J@I          J         1,X10     CC
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@J@ITDATET    L,U       A0,':'            . CHECK FOCD
)@@G@@R FORMAT ERROR    @ @J@I          TE,S3     A0,FIELD1 @D@J@I          J CE
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FORMAT ERROR  @ @J@I          TE,S6     A0,FCF
)@@G@@IELD1 @D@J@I          J         0,X10             . FORMAT ERROR  @^@J@ICG
)@@G@@          LN,U      A2,1@ @J@I          L,U       A3,23     @D@J@I      CH
)@@G@@    L,S1      A0,FIELD1         . CONVERT 'HH'  @ @J@I          AN,U    CI
)@@G@@  A0,'0'    @ @J@I          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @J@I          L,S2    CJ
)@@G@@  A1,FIELD1 @ @J@I          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @J@I          A       CK
)@@G@@  A0,A1     @F@J@I          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHICL
)@@G@@N LIMITS    @D@J@I          J         0,X10             . NO, ERROR     CM
)@@G@@@E@J@I          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @J@ICN
)@@G@@          L,U       A3,59     @D@J@I          L,S4      A0,FIELD1       CO
)@@G@@  . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @J@I          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @J@I          MSCP
)@@G@@I,U     A0,10     @ @J@I          L,S5      A1,FIELD1 @ @J@I          ANCQ
)@@G@@,U      A1,'0'    @ @J@I          A         A0,A1     @F@J@I          TWCR
)@@G@@        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@J@I          J CS
)@@G@@        0,X10             . NO, ERROR     @E@J@I          S,S2      A0,TCT
)@@G@@DATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@J@I          L,S1      A0,FIELD1+CU
)@@G@@1       . CONVERT 'SS'  @ @J@I          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @J@I      CV
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A0,10     @A@J@I          L,S2      A1,FIELD1+1     @ @J@ICW
